### 2. Ethanâ€™s needs being â€œjealously metâ€

## Things to watch so it doesnâ€™t collapse

### 1. Donâ€™t let Ethan become a prop

**Robyn:**

Claire has an epiphany. She realises that it was mostly her insistence on him wearing Emma's jeans that had set this ball in motion. That night, in bed, she begins to imagine Ethan as a girl. Conflicting feelings unsettle her: on one side, guilt. But on the other, the same feelings that fuel Zoe's efforts now consume her... it quickly overwhelms any guilt. It becomes an obsession. She decides to try to gain entry into the girls' conspiratorial activities by promising to be a strong ally and to work on convincing Ethan to abandon boyhood altogether. He looks so happy, so relaxed. He needs to accept their intentions for him.

**Robyn:**

Maya and Zoe have a chat in the library about Zoe's encounter with 'Eve" in the girls' restroom. Maya is a bit taken aback, but realises that she herself had put 'Eve' in second place to Zoe.
